##### getAta()

```ts
getAta(): {
  FanSpeed:   | null
     | auto
     | fast
     | moderate
     | slow
     | very_fast
     | very_slow;
  OperationMode: null | OperationMode;
  Power: null | boolean;
  SetTemperature: null | number;
  VaneHorizontalDirection: null | Horizontal;
  VaneHorizontalSwing: null | boolean;
  VaneVerticalDirection: null | Vertical;
  VaneVerticalSwing: null | boolean;
}
```

     | slow
     | very_fast
     | very_slow;
  OperationMode: null | OperationMode;
  Power: null | boolean;
  SetTemperature: null | number;

  VaneHorizontalSwing: null | boolean;

  VaneVerticalSwing: null | boolean;
}
